 to bury chan .

 a cold tingle ran down della 's spine . 
 was it a ghost ?

 * * * thirty minutes later , the grave dug , della sat on green winter grass , running her hands over the manicured blades and watching the backhoe pull chan 's casket from the ground .

 chapter nine della 's heart did a double tumble before fixing her eyes on the open casket and possibly a decomposed body that she might have to remove .
